- [香奈美](./419_page.md "香奈美")

- 语音
- [誓约](./30338_page.md "香奈美/誓约")

![AI.svg](https://patchwiki.biligame.com/images/klbq/thumb/3/3b/ptlz9hnn4gd0pngltj2gqglwmzb587x.svg/35px-AI.svg.png) 角色台词由[千问ASR模型](http://game.bilibili.com/linkfilter/?url=https://www.modelscope.cn/models/Qwen/Qwen3-ASR-1.7B)和[whisperASR模型](http://game.bilibili.com/linkfilter/?url=https://www.modelscope.cn/models/openai-mirror/whisper-large-v3)听写配合人工后期校对编写，如有错误欢迎[修改指正](./14357_page.md)。
